[1;24r[21;1H[36m# option.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Huse_localtime=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Activate logging of uploads/downloads.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hxferlog_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Make sure PORT transfer connections originate from port 20 (ftp-data).
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hconnect_from_port_20=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# If you want, you can arrange for uploaded anonymous files to be owned by
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# a different user. Note! Using "root" for uploaded files is not
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# recommended!
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chown_uploads=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chown_username=whoever
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may override where the log file goes if you like. The default is shown
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# below.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#xferlog_file=/var/log/vsftpd.log
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# If you want, you can have your log file in standard ftpd xferlog format.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Note that the default log file location is /var/log/xferlog in this case.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#xferlog_std_format=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may change the default value for timing out an idle session.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[C[?12l[?25h[?25lxferlog_std_format=YES[K
[?12l[?25h[?25l[20d[?12l[?25h[?25l[21d[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#idle_session_timeout=600
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may change the default value for timing out a data connection.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#data_connection_timeout=120
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# It is recommended that you define on your system a unique user which the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# ftp server can use as a totally isolated and unprivileged user.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#nopriv_user=ftpsecure
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Enable this and the server will recognise asynchronous ABOR requests. Not
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# recommended for security (the code is non-trivial). Not enabling it,
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# however, may confuse older FTP clients.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#async_abor_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# By default the server will pretend to allow ASCII mode but in fact ignore
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the request. Turn on the below options to have the server actually do ASCII
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# mangling on files when in ASCII mode.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Beware that on some FTP servers, ASCII support allows a denial of service
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# attack (DoS) via the command "SIZE /big/file" in ASCII mode. vsftpd
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# predicted this attack and has always been safe, reporting the size of the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# raw file.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# ASCII mangling is a horrible feature of the protocol.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ascii_upload_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ascii_download_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may fully customise the login banner string:
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ftpd_banner=Welcome to blah FTP service.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may specify a file of disallowed anonymous e-mail addresses. Apparently
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# useful for combatting certain DoS attacks.

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may restrict local users to their home directories.  See the FAQ for
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chroot_local_user=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may specify an explicit list of local users to chroot() to their home
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# directory. If chroot_local_user is YES, then this list becomes a list of
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# users to NOT chroot().
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chroot_list_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# (default follows)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chroot_list_file=/etc/vsftpd.chroot_list
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may activate the "-R" option to the builtin ls. This is disabled by
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# default to avoid remote users being able to cause excessive I/O on large
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Customization
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# This option should be the name of a directory which is empty.  Also, the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# directory should not be writable by the ftp user. This directory is used
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# This string is the name of the PAM service vsftpd will use.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hpam_service_name=vsftpd
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# This option specifies the location of the RSA certificate to use for SSL
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

# Example config file /etc/vsftpd.conf
#
# The default compiled in settings are fairly paranoid. This sample file
# loosens things up a bit, to make the ftp daemon more usable.
# Please see vsftpd.conf.5 for all compiled in defaults.
#
# READ THIS: This example file is NOT an exhaustive list of vsftpd options.
# Please read the vsftpd.conf.5 manual page to get a full idea of vsftpd's
# capabilities.
#
#
# Run standalone?  vsftpd can run either from an inetd or as a standalone
# daemon started from an initscript.
listen=NO
#
# This directive enables listening on IPv6 sockets. By default, listening
# on the IPv6 "any" address (::) will accept connections from both IPv6
# and IPv4 clients. It is not necessary to listen on *both* IPv4 and IPv6
# sockets. If you want that (perhaps because you want to listen on specific
# addresses) then you must run two copies of vsftpd with two configuration
# files.
listen_ipv6=YES
#
# Allow anonymous FTP? (Disabled by default).
anonymous_enable=NO
#
# Uncomment this to allow local users to log in.
local_enable=YES
#
# Uncomment this to enable any form of FTP write command.
#write_enable=YES
#
# Default umask for local users is 077. You may wish to change this to 022,
# if your users expect that (022 is used by most other ftpd's)
local_umask=022
#
# Uncomment this to allow the anonymous FTP user to upload files. This only
# has an effect if the above global write enable is activated. Also, you will
# obviously need to create a directory writable by the FTP user.
#anon_upload_enable=YES
#
# Uncomment this if you want the anonymous FTP user to be able to create
# new directories.
#anon_mkdir_write_enable=YES
#
# Activate directory messages - messages given to remote users when they
# go into a certain directory.
dirmessage_enable=YES
#
# If enabled, vsftpd will display directory listings with the time
# in  your  local  time  zone.  The default is to display GMT. The
# times returned by the MDTM FTP command are also affected by this
# option.
use_localtime=YES
#
# Activate logging of uploads/downloads.
xferlog_enable=YES
#
# Make sure PORT transfer connections originate from port 20 (ftp-data).
connect_from_port_20=YES
#
# If you want, you can arrange for uploaded anonymous files to be owned by
# a different user. Note! Using "root" for uploaded files is not
# recommended!
#chown_uploads=YES
#chown_username=whoever
#
# You may override where the log file goes if you like. The default is shown
# below.
#xferlog_file=/var/log/vsftpd.log
#
# If you want, you can have your log file in standard ftpd xferlog format.
# Note that the default log file location is /var/log/xferlog in this case.
xferlog_std_format=YES
#
# You may change the default value for timing out an idle session.
#idle_session_timeout=600
#
# You may change the default value for timing out a data connection.
#data_connection_timeout=120
#
# It is recommended that you define on your system a unique user which the
# ftp server can use as a totally isolated and unprivileged user.
#nopriv_user=ftpsecure
#
# Enable this and the server will recognise asynchronous ABOR requests. Not
# recommended for security (the code is non-trivial). Not enabling it,
# however, may confuse older FTP clients.
#async_abor_enable=YES
#
# By default the server will pretend to allow ASCII mode but in fact ignore
# the request. Turn on the below options to have the server actually do ASCII
# mangling on files when in ASCII mode.
# Beware that on some FTP servers, ASCII support allows a denial of service
# attack (DoS) via the command "SIZE /big/file" in ASCII mode. vsftpd
# predicted this attack and has always been safe, reporting the size of the
# raw file.
# ASCII mangling is a horrible feature of the protocol.
#ascii_upload_enable=YES
#ascii_download_enable=YES
#
# You may fully customise the login banner string:
#ftpd_banner=Welcome to blah FTP service.
#
# You may specify a file of disallowed anonymous e-mail addresses. Apparently
# useful for combatting certain DoS attacks.
#deny_email_enable=YES
# (default follows)
#banned_email_file=/etc/vsftpd.banned_emails
#
# You may restrict local users to their home directories.  See the FAQ for
# the possible risks in this before using chroot_local_user or
# chroot_list_enable below.
chroot_local_user=YES
#
# You may specify an explicit list of local users to chroot() to their home
# directory. If chroot_local_user is YES, then this list becomes a list of
# users to NOT chroot().
# (Warning! chroot'ing can be very dangerous. If using chroot, make sure that
# the user does not have write access to the top level directory within the
# chroot)
chroot_local_user=YES
#chroot_list_enable=YES
# (default follows)
#chroot_list_file=/etc/vsftpd.chroot_list
#
# You may activate the "-R" option to the builtin ls. This is disabled by
# default to avoid remote users being able to cause excessive I/O on large
# sites. However, some broken FTP clients such as "ncftp" and "mirror" assume
# the presence of the "-R" option, so there is a strong case for enabling it.
#ls_recurse_enable=YES
#
# Customization
#
# Some of vsftpd's settings don't fit the filesystem layout by
# default.
#
# This option should be the name of a directory which is empty.  Also, the
# directory should not be writable by the ftp user. This directory is used
# as a secure chroot() jail at times vsftpd does not require filesystem
# access.
secure_chroot_dir=/var/run/vsftpd/empty
#
# This string is the name of the PAM service vsftpd will use.
pam_service_name=vsftpd
#
# This option specifies the location of the RSA certificate to use for SSL
# encrypted connections.
rsa_cert_file=/etc/ssl/certs/ssl-cert-snakeoil.pem
rsa_private_key_file=/etc/ssl/private/ssl-cert-snakeoil.key
ssl_enable=NO

#
# Uncomment this to indicate that vsftpd use a utf8 filesystem.
#utf8_filesystem=YES

[22d[2d[39;49m[36m# Example config file /etc/vsftpd.conf
[3d#[4d# The default compiled in settings are fairly paranoid. This sample file
[5d# loosens things up a bit, to make the ftp daemon more usable.
[6d# Please see vsftpd.conf.5 for all compiled in defaults.
[7d#[8d# READ THIS: This example file is NOT an exhaustive list of vsftpd options.
[9d# Please read the vsftpd.conf.5 manual page to get a full idea of vsftpd's
[10d# capabilities.
[11d#[12d#[13d# Run standalone?  vsftpd can run either from an inetd or as a standalone
[14d# daemon started from an initscript.
[15d[39m(B[mlisten=NO
[16d[36m#[17d# This directive enables listening on IPv6 sockets. By default, listening
[18d# on the IPv6 "any" address (::) will accept connections from both IPv6
[19d# and IPv4 clients. It is not necessary to listen on *both* IPv4 and IPv6
[20d# sockets. If you want that (perhaps because you want to listen on specific
[21d# addresses) then you must run two copies of vsftpd with two configuration
[2d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[4d[?12l[?25h[?25l[5d[?12l[?25h[?25l[6d[?12l[?25h[?25l[7d[?12l[?25h[?25l[8d[?12l[?25h[?25l[9d[?12l[?25h[?25l[10d[?12l[?25h[?25l[11d[?12l[?25h[?25l[12d[?12l[?25h[?25l[13d[?12l[?25h[?25l[14d[?12l[?25h[?25l[15d[?12l[?25h[?25l[16d[?12l[?25h[?25l[17d[?12l[?25h[?25l[18d[?12l[?25h[?25l[19d[?12l[?25h[?25l[20d[?12l[?25h[?25l[21d[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# files.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1Hlisten_ipv6=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Allow anonymous FTP? (Disabled by default).
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1Hanonymous_enable=NO
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to allow local users to log in.[39m(B[m[K
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hlocal_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to enable any form of FTP write command.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#write_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Default umask for local users is 077. You may wish to change this to 022,
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# if your users expect that (022 is used by most other ftpd's)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hlocal_umask=022
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to allow the anonymous FTP user to upload files. This only
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# has an effect if the above global write enable is activated. Also, you will
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# obviously need to create a directory writable by the FTP user.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#anon_upload_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this if you want the anonymous FTP user to be able to create
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# new directories.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#anon_mkdir_write_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Activate directory messages - messages given to remote users when they
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# go into a certain directory.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hdirmessage_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# If enabled, vsftpd will display directory listings with the time
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# in  your  local  time  zone.  The default is to display GMT. The
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# times returned by the MDTM FTP command are also affected by this
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# option.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Huse_localtime=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Activate logging of uploads/downloads.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hxferlog_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Make sure PORT transfer connections originate from port 20 (ftp-data).
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hconnect_from_port_20=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# If you want, you can arrange for uploaded anonymous files to be owned by
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# a different user. Note! Using "root" for uploaded files is not
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# recommended!
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chown_uploads=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chown_username=whoever
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may override where the log file goes if you like. The default is shown
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# below.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#xferlog_file=/var/log/vsftpd.log
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# If you want, you can have your log file in standard ftpd xferlog format.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Note that the default log file location is /var/log/xferlog in this case.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hxferlog_std_format=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may change the default value for timing out an idle session.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#idle_session_timeout=600
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may change the default value for timing out a data connection.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#data_connection_timeout=120
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# It is recommended that you define on your system a unique user which the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# ftp server can use as a totally isolated and unprivileged user.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#nopriv_user=ftpsecure
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Enable this and the server will recognise asynchronous ABOR requests. Not
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# recommended for security (the code is non-trivial). Not enabling it,
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# however, may confuse older FTP clients.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#async_abor_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# By default the server will pretend to allow ASCII mode but in fact ignore
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the request. Turn on the below options to have the server actually do ASCII
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# mangling on files when in ASCII mode.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Beware that on some FTP servers, ASCII support allows a denial of service
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# attack (DoS) via the command "SIZE /big/file" in ASCII mode. vsftpd
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# predicted this attack and has always been safe, reporting the size of the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# raw file.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# ASCII mangling is a horrible feature of the protocol.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ascii_upload_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ascii_download_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may fully customise the login banner string:
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ftpd_banner=Welcome to blah FTP service.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may specify a file of disallowed anonymous e-mail addresses. Apparently
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# useful for combatting certain DoS attacks.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#deny_email_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# (default follows)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#banned_email_file=/etc/vsftpd.banned_emails
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may restrict local users to their home directories.  See the FAQ for
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the possible risks in this before using chroot_local_user or
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# chroot_list_enable below.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hchroot_local_user=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may specify an explicit list of local users to chroot() to their home
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# directory. If chroot_local_user is YES, then this list becomes a list of
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# users to NOT chroot().
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# (Warning! chroot'ing can be very dangerous. If using chroot, make sure that
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the user does not have write access to the top level directory within the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# chroot)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hchroot_local_user=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chroot_list_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# (default follows)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chroot_list_file=/etc/vsftpd.chroot_list
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may activate the "-R" option to the builtin ls. This is disabled by
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[21d# default to avoid remote users being able to cause excessive I/O on large[21;25H[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8
[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# sites. However, some broken FTP clients such as "ncftp" and "mirror" assume
[20d# the presence of the "-R" option, so there is a strong case for enabling it.
[21d#ls_recurse_enable=YES[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8
[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m#[20d# Customization
[21d#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# Some of vsftpd's settings don't fit the filesystem layout by
[20d# default.
[21d#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[6S[1;24r[16;1H[36m# This option should be the name of a directory which is empty.  Also, the
[17d# directory should not be writable by the ftp user. This directory is used
[18d# as a secure chroot() jail at times vsftpd does not require filesystem
[19d# access.
[20d[39m(B[msecure_chroot_dir=/var/run/vsftpd/empty
[21d[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# This string is the name of the PAM service vsftpd will use.
[20d[39m(B[mpam_service_name=vsftpd
[21d[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# This option specifies the location of the RSA certificate to use for SSL
[20d# encrypted connections.
[21d[39m(B[mrsa_cert_file=/etc/ssl/certs/ssl-cert-snakeoil.pem[21;25H[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8
[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1Hrsa_private_key_file=/etc/ssl/private/ssl-cert-snakeoil.key
[20dssl_enable=NO
[21d[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m#[20d# Uncomment this to indicate that vsftpd use a utf8 filesystem.
[21d#utf8_filesystem=YES[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8

[22d[2d[39;49m[36m# Example config file /etc/vsftpd.conf
[3d#[4d# The default compiled in settings are fairly paranoid. This sample file
[5d# loosens things up a bit, to make the ftp daemon more usable.
[6d# Please see vsftpd.conf.5 for all compiled in defaults.
[7d#[8d# READ THIS: This example file is NOT an exhaustive list of vsftpd options.
[9d# Please read the vsftpd.conf.5 manual page to get a full idea of vsftpd's
[10d# capabilities.
[11d#[12d#[13d# Run standalone?  vsftpd can run either from an inetd or as a standalone
[14d# daemon started from an initscript.
[15d[39m(B[mlisten=NO
[16d[36m#[17d# This directive enables listening on IPv6 sockets. By default, listening
[18d# on the IPv6 "any" address (::) will accept connections from both IPv6
[19d# and IPv4 clients. It is not necessary to listen on *both* IPv4 and IPv6
[20d# sockets. If you want that (perhaps because you want to listen on specific
[21d# addresses) then you must run two copies of vsftpd with two configuration
[2d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[4d[?12l[?25h[?25l[5d[?12l[?25h[?25l[6d[?12l[?25h[?25l[7d[?12l[?25h[?25l[8d[?12l[?25h[?25l[9d[?12l[?25h[?25l[10d[?12l[?25h[?25l[11d[?12l[?25h[?25l[12d[?12l[?25h[?25l[13d[?12l[?25h[?25l[14d[?12l[?25h[?25l[15d[?12l[?25h[?25l[16d[?12l[?25h[?25l[17d[?12l[?25h[?25l[18d[?12l[?25h[?25l[19d[?12l[?25h[?25l[20d[?12l[?25h[?25l[21d[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# files.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1Hlisten_ipv6=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Allow anonymous FTP? (Disabled by default).
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1Hanonymous_enable=NO
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to allow local users to log in.[39m(B[m[K
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hlocal_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to enable any form of FTP write command.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#write_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Default umask for local users is 077. You may wish to change this to 022,
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# if your users expect that (022 is used by most other ftpd's)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hlocal_umask=022
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to allow the anonymous FTP user to upload files. This only
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# has an effect if the above global write enable is activated. Also, you will
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# obviously need to create a directory writable by the FTP user.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#anon_upload_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this if you want the anonymous FTP user to be able to create
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# new directories.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#anon_mkdir_write_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Activate directory messages - messages given to remote users when they
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# go into a certain directory.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hdirmessage_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# If enabled, vsftpd will display directory listings with the time
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# in  your  local  time  zone.  The default is to display GMT. The
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# times returned by the MDTM FTP command are also affected by this
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# option.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Huse_localtime=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Activate logging of uploads/downloads.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hxferlog_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Make sure PORT transfer connections originate from port 20 (ftp-data).
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hconnect_from_port_20=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# If you want, you can arrange for uploaded anonymous files to be owned by
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# a different user. Note! Using "root" for uploaded files is not
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# recommended!
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chown_uploads=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chown_username=whoever
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may override where the log file goes if you like. The default is shown
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# below.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#xferlog_file=/var/log/vsftpd.log
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# If you want, you can have your log file in standard ftpd xferlog format.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Note that the default log file location is /var/log/xferlog in this case.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hxferlog_std_format=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may change the default value for timing out an idle session.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#idle_session_timeout=600
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may change the default value for timing out a data connection.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#data_connection_timeout=120
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# It is recommended that you define on your system a unique user which the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# ftp server can use as a totally isolated and unprivileged user.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#nopriv_user=ftpsecure
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Enable this and the server will recognise asynchronous ABOR requests. Not
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# recommended for security (the code is non-trivial). Not enabling it,
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# however, may confuse older FTP clients.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#async_abor_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# By default the server will pretend to allow ASCII mode but in fact ignore
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the request. Turn on the below options to have the server actually do ASCII
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# mangling on files when in ASCII mode.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Beware that on some FTP servers, ASCII support allows a denial of service
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# attack (DoS) via the command "SIZE /big/file" in ASCII mode. vsftpd
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# predicted this attack and has always been safe, reporting the size of the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# raw file.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# ASCII mangling is a horrible feature of the protocol.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ascii_upload_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ascii_download_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may fully customise the login banner string:
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ftpd_banner=Welcome to blah FTP service.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may specify a file of disallowed anonymous e-mail addresses. Apparently
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# useful for combatting certain DoS attacks.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#deny_email_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# (default follows)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#banned_email_file=/etc/vsftpd.banned_emails
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may restrict local users to their home directories.  See the FAQ for
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the possible risks in this before using chroot_local_user or
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# chroot_list_enable below.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hchroot_local_user=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may specify an explicit list of local users to chroot() to their home
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# directory. If chroot_local_user is YES, then this list becomes a list of
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# users to NOT chroot().
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# (Warning! chroot'ing can be very dangerous. If using chroot, make sure that
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the user does not have write access to the top level directory within the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# chroot)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hchroot_local_user=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[22d[2d[39;49m[36m# Example config file /etc/vsftpd.conf
[3d#[4d# The default compiled in settings are fairly paranoid. This sample file
[5d# loosens things up a bit, to make the ftp daemon more usable.
[6d# Please see vsftpd.conf.5 for all compiled in defaults.
[7d#[8d# READ THIS: This example file is NOT an exhaustive list of vsftpd options.
[9d# Please read the vsftpd.conf.5 manual page to get a full idea of vsftpd's
[10d# capabilities.
[11d#[12d#[13d# Run standalone?  vsftpd can run either from an inetd or as a standalone
[14d# daemon started from an initscript.
[15d[39m(B[mlisten=NO
[16d[36m#[17d# This directive enables listening on IPv6 sockets. By default, listening
[18d# on the IPv6 "any" address (::) will accept connections from both IPv6
[19d# and IPv4 clients. It is not necessary to listen on *both* IPv4 and IPv6
[20d# sockets. If you want that (perhaps because you want to listen on specific
[21d# addresses) then you must run two copies of vsftpd with two configuration
[2d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[4d[?12l[?25h[?25l[5d[?12l[?25h[?25l[6d[?12l[?25h[?25l[7d[?12l[?25h[?25l[8d[?12l[?25h[?25l[9d[?12l[?25h[?25l[10d[?12l[?25h[?25l[11d[?12l[?25h[?25l[12d[?12l[?25h[?25l[13d[?12l[?25h[?25l[14d[?12l[?25h[?25l[15d[?12l[?25h[?25l[16d[?12l[?25h[?25l[17d[?12l[?25h[?25l[18d[?12l[?25h[?25l[19d[?12l[?25h[?25l[20d[?12l[?25h[?25l[21d[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# files.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1Hlisten_ipv6=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Allow anonymous FTP? (Disabled by default).
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1Hanonymous_enable=NO
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to allow local users to log in.[39m(B[m[K
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hlocal_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to enable any form of FTP write command.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#write_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Default umask for local users is 077. You may wish to change this to 022,
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# if your users expect that (022 is used by most other ftpd's)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hlocal_umask=022
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to allow the anonymous FTP user to upload files. This only
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# has an effect if the above global write enable is activated. Also, you will
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# obviously need to create a directory writable by the FTP user.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#anon_upload_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this if you want the anonymous FTP user to be able to create
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# new directories.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#anon_mkdir_write_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Activate directory messages - messages given to remote users when they
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# go into a certain directory.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# If enabled, vsftpd will display directory listings with the time
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# in  your  local  time  zone.  The default is to display GMT. The
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Huse_localtime=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Activate logging of uploads/downloads.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hxferlog_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Make sure PORT transfer connections originate from port 20 (ftp-data).
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hconnect_from_port_20=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# If you want, you can arrange for uploaded anonymous files to be owned by
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# a different user. Note! Using "root" for uploaded files is not
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# recommended!
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may override where the log file goes if you like. The default is shown

[1;24r[21;1H[36m# If you want, you can have your log file in standard ftpd xferlog format.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Note that the default log file location is /var/log/xferlog in this case.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hxferlog_std_format=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[1;24r[21;1H[36m# It is recommended that you define on your system a unique user which the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Enable this and the server will recognise asynchronous ABOR requests. Not
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# recommended for security (the code is non-trivial). Not enabling it,
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# however, may confuse older FTP clients.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#async_abor_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# By default the server will pretend to allow ASCII mode but in fact ignore
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the request. Turn on the below options to have the server actually do ASCII
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# mangling on files when in ASCII mode.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Beware that on some FTP servers, ASCII support allows a denial of service
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# attack (DoS) via the command "SIZE /big/file" in ASCII mode. vsftpd
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# predicted this attack and has always been safe, reporting the size of the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# raw file.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# ASCII mangling is a horrible feature of the protocol.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ascii_upload_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ascii_download_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may fully customise the login banner string:
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ftpd_banner=Welcome to blah FTP service.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may specify a file of disallowed anonymous e-mail addresses. Apparently
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# useful for combatting certain DoS attacks.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#deny_email_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# (default follows)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#banned_email_file=/etc/vsftpd.banned_emails
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may restrict local users to their home directories.  See the FAQ for
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the possible risks in this before using chroot_local_user or
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# chroot_list_enable below.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hchroot_local_user=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hallow_writable_chroot=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may specify an explicit list of local users to chroot() to their home
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# directory. If chroot_local_user is YES, then this list becomes a list of
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# users to NOT chroot().
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# (Warning! chroot'ing can be very dangerous. If using chroot, make sure that
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the user does not have write access to the top level directory within the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# chroot)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chroot_local_user=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chroot_list_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# (default follows)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chroot_list_file=/etc/vsftpd.chroot_list
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may activate the "-R" option to the builtin ls. This is disabled by
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[8d[?12l[?25h[?25l[9d[?12l[?25h[?25l[10d[?12l[?25h[?25l[11d[?12l[?25h[?25l[12d[?12l[?25h[?25l[13d[?12l[?25h[?25l[14d[?12l[?25h[?25l[15d[?12l[?25h[?25l[16d[?12l[?25h[?25l[C[?12l[?25h[?25l[1;71H(B[0;7mModified(B[m
[16dchroot_local_user=YES[K
[?12l[?25h[?25lc[?12l[?25h[?25l[17d[?12l[?25h[?25l[18d[?12l[?25h[?25l[19d[?12l[?25h[?25l[20d[?12l[?25h[?25l[21d[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# default to avoid remote users being able to cause excessive I/O on large
#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# sites. However, some broken FTP clients such as "ncftp" and "mirror" assume
#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the presence of the "-R" option, so there is a strong case for enabling it.
#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ls_recurse_enable=YES

[22d[2d[39;49m[36m# Example config file /etc/vsftpd.conf
[3d#[4d# The default compiled in settings are fairly paranoid. This sample file
[5d# loosens things up a bit, to make the ftp daemon more usable.
[6d# Please see vsftpd.conf.5 for all compiled in defaults.
[7d#[8d# READ THIS: This example file is NOT an exhaustive list of vsftpd options.
[9d# Please read the vsftpd.conf.5 manual page to get a full idea of vsftpd's
[10d# capabilities.
[11d#[12d#[13d# Run standalone?  vsftpd can run either from an inetd or as a standalone
[14d# daemon started from an initscript.
[15d[39m(B[mlisten=NO
[16d[36m#[17d# This directive enables listening on IPv6 sockets. By default, listening
[18d# on the IPv6 "any" address (::) will accept connections from both IPv6
[19d# and IPv4 clients. It is not necessary to listen on *both* IPv4 and IPv6
[20d# sockets. If you want that (perhaps because you want to listen on specific
[21d# addresses) then you must run two copies of vsftpd with two configuration
[2d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[4d[?12l[?25h[?25l[5d[?12l[?25h[?25l[6d[?12l[?25h[?25l[7d[?12l[?25h[?25l[8d[?12l[?25h[?25l[9d[?12l[?25h[?25l[10d[?12l[?25h[?25l[11d[?12l[?25h[?25l[12d[?12l[?25h[?25l[13d[?12l[?25h[?25l[14d[?12l[?25h[?25l[15d[?12l[?25h[?25l[16d[?12l[?25h[?25l[17d[?12l[?25h[?25l[18d[?12l[?25h[?25l[19d[?12l[?25h[?25l[20d[?12l[?25h[?25l[21d[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# files.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1Hlisten_ipv6=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Allow anonymous FTP? (Disabled by default).
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1Hanonymous_enable=NO
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to allow local users to log in.[39m(B[m[K
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hlocal_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to enable any form of FTP write command.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#write_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Default umask for local users is 077. You may wish to change this to 022,
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# if your users expect that (022 is used by most other ftpd's)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hlocal_umask=022
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to allow the anonymous FTP user to upload files. This only
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# has an effect if the above global write enable is activated. Also, you will
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# obviously need to create a directory writable by the FTP user.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#anon_upload_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this if you want the anonymous FTP user to be able to create
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#anon_mkdir_write_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Activate directory messages - messages given to remote users when they
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# in  your  local  time  zone.  The default is to display GMT. The
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[1;24r[21;1Huse_localtime=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Activate logging of uploads/downloads.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hxferlog_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Make sure PORT transfer connections originate from port 20 (ftp-data).
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hconnect_from_port_20=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# If you want, you can arrange for uploaded anonymous files to be owned by
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# a different user. Note! Using "root" for uploaded files is not
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# recommended!
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chown_uploads=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chown_username=whoever
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Huserlist_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Huserlist_file=etc/vsftpd.userlist
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may override where the log file goes if you like. The default is shown
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# below.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#xferlog_file=/var/log/vsftpd.log
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# If you want, you can have your log file in standard ftpd xferlog format.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Note that the default log file location is /var/log/xferlog in this case.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hxferlog_std_format=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may change the default value for timing out an idle session.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#idle_session_timeout=600
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may change the default value for timing out a data connection.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#data_connection_timeout=120
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# It is recommended that you define on your system a unique user which the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# ftp server can use as a totally isolated and unprivileged user.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#nopriv_user=ftpsecure
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Enable this and the server will recognise asynchronous ABOR requests. Not
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# recommended for security (the code is non-trivial). Not enabling it,
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# however, may confuse older FTP clients.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#async_abor_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# By default the server will pretend to allow ASCII mode but in fact ignore
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the request. Turn on the below options to have the server actually do ASCII
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# mangling on files when in ASCII mode.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Beware that on some FTP servers, ASCII support allows a denial of service
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# attack (DoS) via the command "SIZE /big/file" in ASCII mode. vsftpd
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# predicted this attack and has always been safe, reporting the size of the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# raw file.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# ASCII mangling is a horrible feature of the protocol.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ascii_upload_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ascii_download_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may fully customise the login banner string:
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ftpd_banner=Welcome to blah FTP service.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may specify a file of disallowed anonymous e-mail addresses. Apparently
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# useful for combatting certain DoS attacks.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#deny_email_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# (default follows)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#banned_email_file=/etc/vsftpd.banned_emails
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may restrict local users to their home directories.  See the FAQ for
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the possible risks in this before using chroot_local_user or
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# chroot_list_enable below.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hchroot_local_user=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hallow_writable_chroot=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may specify an explicit list of local users to chroot() to their home
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# directory. If chroot_local_user is YES, then this list becomes a list of
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# users to NOT chroot().
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# (Warning! chroot'ing can be very dangerous. If using chroot, make sure that
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the user does not have write access to the top level directory within the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# chroot)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hchroot_local_user=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chroot_list_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# (default follows)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#chroot_list_file=/etc/vsftpd.chroot_list
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may activate the "-R" option to the builtin ls. This is disabled by
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# default to avoid remote users being able to cause excessive I/O on large
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# sites. However, some broken FTP clients such as "ncftp" and "mirror" assume
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the presence of the "-R" option, so there is a strong case for enabling it.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#ls_recurse_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Customization
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Some of vsftpd's settings don't fit the filesystem layout by
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# default.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# This option should be the name of a directory which is empty.  Also, the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# directory should not be writable by the ftp user. This directory is used
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# as a secure chroot() jail at times vsftpd does not require filesystem
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# access.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hsecure_chroot_dir=/var/run/vsftpd/empty
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# This string is the name of the PAM service vsftpd will use.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hpam_service_name=vsftpd
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# This option specifies the location of the RSA certificate to use for SSL
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# encrypted connections.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hrsa_private_key_file=/etc/ssl/private/ssl-cert-snakeoil.key
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1Hssl_enable=NO
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to indicate that vsftpd use a utf8 filesystem.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Enable this and the server will recognise asynchronous ABOR requests. Not
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# By default the server will pretend to allow ASCII mode but in fact ignore
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# the request. Turn on the below options to have the server actually do ASCII
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# mangling on files when in ASCII mode.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Beware that on some FTP servers, ASCII support allows a denial of service
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# attack (DoS) via the command "SIZE /big/file" in ASCII mode. vsftpd
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# predicted this attack and has always been safe, reporting the size of the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# raw file.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# ASCII mangling is a horrible feature of the protocol.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may fully customise the login banner string:

[1;24r[21;1H[36m# You may specify a file of disallowed anonymous e-mail addresses. Apparently

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# This option should be the name of a directory which is empty.  Also, the
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[22d[2d[39;49m[36m# Example config file /etc/vsftpd.conf
[3d#[4d# The default compiled in settings are fairly paranoid. This sample file
[5d# loosens things up a bit, to make the ftp daemon more usable.
[6d# Please see vsftpd.conf.5 for all compiled in defaults.
[7d#[8d# READ THIS: This example file is NOT an exhaustive list of vsftpd options.
[9d# Please read the vsftpd.conf.5 manual page to get a full idea of vsftpd's
[10d# capabilities.
[11d#[12d#[13d# Run standalone?  vsftpd can run either from an inetd or as a standalone
[14d# daemon started from an initscript.
[15d[39m(B[mlisten=NO
[16d[36m#[17d# This directive enables listening on IPv6 sockets. By default, listening
[18d# on the IPv6 "any" address (::) will accept connections from both IPv6
[19d# and IPv4 clients. It is not necessary to listen on *both* IPv4 and IPv6
[20d# sockets. If you want that (perhaps because you want to listen on specific
[21d# addresses) then you must run two copies of vsftpd with two configuration
[2d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[4d[?12l[?25h[?25l[5d[?12l[?25h[?25l[6d[?12l[?25h[?25l[7d[?12l[?25h[?25l[8d[?12l[?25h[?25l[9d[?12l[?25h[?25l[10d[?12l[?25h[?25l[11d[?12l[?25h[?25l[12d[?12l[?25h[?25l[13d[?12l[?25h[?25l[14d[?12l[?25h[?25l[15d[?12l[?25h[?25l[16d[?12l[?25h[?25l[17d[?12l[?25h[?25l[18d[?12l[?25h[?25l[19d[?12l[?25h[?25l[20d[?12l[?25h[?25l[21d[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# files.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1Hlisten_ipv6=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Allow anonymous FTP? (Disabled by default).
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1Hanonymous_enable=NO
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#write_enable=YES

[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Default umask for local users is 077. You may wish to change this to 022,
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# if your users expect that (022 is used by most other ftpd's)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this to allow the anonymous FTP user to upload files. This only
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# has an effect if the above global write enable is activated. Also, you will
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m#anon_upload_enable=YES

[1;24r[21;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d
[1;24r[21;1H[36m# Uncomment this if you want the anonymous FTP user to be able to create

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m#[20d# By default the server will pretend to allow ASCII mode but in fact ignore
[21d# the request. Turn on the below options to have the server actually do ASCII
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# mangling on files when in ASCII mode.

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# predicted this attack and has always been safe, reporting the size of the

[20d[36m#chroot_list_enable=YES
[21d# (default follows)

[20d#[21d# You may activate the "-R" option to the builtin ls. This is disabled by
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# default to avoid remote users being able to cause excessive I/O on large

[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m#anon_upload_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# obviously need to create a directory writable by the FTP user.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# has an effect if the above global write enable is activated. Also, you will
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# Uncomment this to allow the anonymous FTP user to upload files. This only
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1Hlocal_umask=022
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# if your users expect that (022 is used by most other ftpd's)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# Default umask for local users is 077. You may wish to change this to 022,
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m#write_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# Uncomment this to enable any form of FTP write command.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1Hlocal_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# Uncomment this to allow local users to log in.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1Hanonymous_enable=NO
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# Allow anonymous FTP? (Disabled by default).
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1Hlisten_ipv6=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# files.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# addresses) then you must run two copies of vsftpd with two configuration
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# sockets. If you want that (perhaps because you want to listen on specific
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# and IPv4 clients. It is not necessary to listen on *both* IPv4 and IPv6
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# on the IPv6 "any" address (::) will accept connections from both IPv6
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# This directive enables listening on IPv6 sockets. By default, listening
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1Hlisten=NO
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# daemon started from an initscript.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# Run standalone?  vsftpd can run either from an inetd or as a standalone
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# capabilities.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# Please read the vsftpd.conf.5 manual page to get a full idea of vsftpd's
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# READ THIS: This example file is NOT an exhaustive list of vsftpd options.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# Please see vsftpd.conf.5 for all compiled in defaults.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# loosens things up a bit, to make the ftp daemon more usable.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# The default compiled in settings are fairly paranoid. This sample file
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;21r8M[1;24r[2;1H[36m# Example config file /etc/vsftpd.conf
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[?12l[?25h[?25l[?12l[?25h[?25l[?12l[?25h[?25l[?12l[?25h[?25l[?12l[?25h[?25l[?12l[?25h[?25l[?12l[?25h[?25l[?12l[?25h[?25l[5d[?12l[?25h[?25l[8d[?12l[?25h[?25l[11d[?12l[?25h[?25l[14d[?12l[?25h[?25l[17d[?12l[?25h[?25l[20d[?12l[?25h[?25l[2;22r[22;1H[2S[1;24r[20;1H[36m# files.
[21d[39m(B[mlisten_ipv6=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m#[20d# Allow anonymous FTP? (Disabled by default).
[21d[39m(B[manonymous_enable=NO
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m#[20d# Uncomment this to allow local users to log in.
[21d[39m(B[mlocal_enable=YES
[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m#[20d# Uncomment this to enable any form of FTP write command.
[21d#write_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m#[20d# Default umask for local users is 077. You may wish to change this to 022,
[21d# if your users expect that (022 is used by most other ftpd's)
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1Hlocal_umask=022
[20d[36m#[21d# Uncomment this to allow the anonymous FTP user to upload files. This only
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# has an effect if the above global write enable is activated. Also, you will
[20d# obviously need to create a directory writable by the FTP user.
[21d#anon_upload_enable=YES
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m#[20d# Uncomment this if you want the anonymous FTP user to be able to create
[21d# new directories.
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m#anon_mkdir_write_enable=YES
[20d#[21d# Activate directory messages - messages given to remote users when they
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# go into a certain directory.
[20d[39m(B[mdirmessage_enable=YES
[21d[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# If enabled, vsftpd will display directory listings with the time
[20d# in  your  local  time  zone.  The default is to display GMT. The
[21d# times returned by the MDTM FTP command are also affected by this
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# option.
[20d[39m(B[muse_localtime=YES
[21d[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# Activate logging of uploads/downloads.
[20d[39m(B[mxferlog_enable=YES
[21d[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# Make sure PORT transfer connections originate from port 20 (ftp-data).
[20d[39m(B[mconnect_from_port_20=YES
[21d[36m#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m# If you want, you can arrange for uploaded anonymous files to be owned by
[20d# a different user. Note! Using "root" for uploaded files is not
[21d# recommended!
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m#chown_uploads=YES
[20d#chown_username=whoever
[21d#[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l7[2;22r8[22d[3S[1;24r[19;1H[36m#userlist_enable=YES
[20d#userlist_file=etc/vsftpd.userlist
[21d#userlist_deny=NO
[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[A[?12l[?25h[?25l[C[?12l[?25h[?25luserlist_enable=YES[K
[?12l[?25h[?25l[20d[?12l[?25h[?25l[C[?12l[?25h[?25luserlist_file=etc/vsftpd.userlist[K
[?12l[?25h[?25l[21d[?12l[?25h[?25l[C[?12l[?25h[?25luserlist_deny=NO[K
